< Text>
I came here during lunch on a Friday. Not very busy. Its small here. 3 booths and 5 tables. Other than pho, they also have Banh Mi, rice entrees, vermicelli, and various boba drinks. I always get pho tai (rare steak) when I hit up vietnamese spots. The pho tai here is pretty good. I got the large which seemed a bit smaller than im used to. The prices seem fair and the service is good. FYI they charge $0.50 if you use a cc for purchases below $5.

Overall good pho with expected price and service. I'll come back when I'm in the area and I'm craving pho.< /Text>

<Name>Pat King< /Name><Review>First let me say that I DO NOT write a lot of reviews, coming from a marketing background I know how badly negative reviews can impact a business and in many cases 1 review/experience is not a realistic snapshot of a business. Everyone has a  bad day and nobody is perfect.

That being said, my experience with this Clinic overall in several experiences is the ABSOLUTE WORST I have had in 25 years dealing with many medical issues.

I have recently relocated to this area and was in desperate need of finding a doctor to treat ongoing chronic health issues. This place was sadly recommended.

Here is a summary of my experience.

-The staff in general is very friendly in all interactions. This is not a cut on them by any means.

-Sharing my health history and what medications that have worked for me was a complete waste of time. I even offered a copy of my medical records that confirm my history. Instead of prescribing me what I had used that was working for me, they unknowingly prescribed me something I never heard of. I didn't know until I went to the pharmacy to pick it up. I was a little confused, but kept an open mind and took the medication anyway.

However, the medication made me very ill. So I called them to see if they could switch my prescription to the other medication that I had been taking. They confirmed that they sent the new prescription to the pharmacy. Upon going to pick it up, I find out that its OTC medication that I had already told them didn't work for me during the visit. I didn't pick up the medication and instead called them yet again and was clear on what I had been prescribed and what didn't work for me. At this point, they made me come in and give urine for an unknown test. They  never even told me what they were testing me for (I can only assume it was a drug test, which I don't care because I do not use any kind of narcotics and certainly wasn't seeking any. After the test, I had to go back to the pharmacy yet again only to find out that they sent the wrong prescription and not properly prescribed which was caught by the pharmacist. 5 more phone calls from me and 2 calls from the pharmacy all while Im there waiting and 5 hours later, I finally got the right medication only after they sent it to a completely different pharmacy that I had never used, in a town where I have never lived. They had my pharmacy on file and had already sent me multiple medications there.

So multiple times they prescribed me something that I wasn't aware of, they were oddly secretive about telling me and let me find out what I went to the pharmacy. ??????

They made me come back to the office to give a urine sample for some kind of test that they never even disclosed to me.

Kept me at the pharmacy for 5 hours and many calls back and forth to finally get my 1 very simple prescription filled. They were unapologetic, very standoffish and not concerned at all with quality customer service or ensuring that I am being properly treated for a serious chronic health condition.

I don't know if the mystery with the different medications is related to prescribing something that they get kick backs for or what. It's all very odd and something I have never experienced. This could all perhaps be a direct result of the physician assistant's incompetence. His name was Mr. White. As I stated, the rest of the staff was very nice and friendly.

Lastly, I asked to have my blood pressure medication filled multiple times and after all this I am still without my blood pressure meds which is not good. How many more hoops would I have to jump through to get another medication? One that is potentially life threatening.....??????

The support staff on the phone at the main office should get some customer service training, learn some compassion and how to come across understanding to the customer (even if they don't understand or agree, fake it).

I will NEVER go back here. Id rather sit in an emergency room all day.</Review><date>1548721526421< /date>< user_id>

< review>
Great addition to PB. Even with a number of existing Thai restaurants, this is a much-needed replacement for the sad diner that once resided here.

The open air and bright location is welcoming, but my review is only based on a takeout experience, so I canâ€™t speak to dining in. I ordered online for pickup at a future time and the experience was seamless. One of the easiest online ordering interfaces Iâ€™ve used and a 15% discount for first-time users.

Initially I was surprised at the reasonable prices, wondering if quality would underwhelm or if portion sizes were small. My food was ready right on time and had definitely not been sitting around for awhile. You can skip the line at the register and the lady at the counter helped me immediately.

My initial concerns vanished before taking the first bite. The food smelled great, portions were substantial, and looked fresh. First bite corroborated reviews from the other locations - itâ€™s delicious. I had the massaman curry with rice and veggies and it was scrumptious. My only qualm is that I wanted it spicy but it was extremely mild. Aside from a weak spice level, the chicken was excellent and curry was very flavorful. My friend ordered the drunken noodle which was equally fresh and delicious.

This is definitely going into my regular takeout rotation. Glad to see this block of Garnet gain another restaurant and I hope it can be successful. It was crowded on a Wednesday evening.</review>

<text>I've been ordering from Fresh Brothers in Hollywood for a few years now, ever since I moved into the neighborhood, and I've noticed a decline in both quality and service.

Several months ago, I ordered a cauliflower crust pizza for delivery. The delivery time was about average, however the pizza was burnt. It was late evening on the weekend, so I didn't bother to reorder.

Just today, I received an email promotion to try their newest pizza. When I tried to order online, I wasn't able to complete the transaction. When I called the shop and explained the situation, I was told that the order did not meet the minimum requirement for delivery, because the coupon code from their email special discounted the total amount to be below the minimum. I asked if they would be able to override this and allow me to order for delivery since the order did exceed the minimum requirement before the coupon, and they said no.

So, long story short, I did not order the pizza. And they did not offer up any other solution. They literally told me that the order did not meet the minimum for delivery, and that was it. With the number of other options in the Hollywood area, I will not be ordering from Fresh Brothers again, nor will I recommend them.

Fresh Brothers, I encourage you to think about your service model from a customer's perspective, and see the experience through their eyes. I also recommend that you consider adding language to both your website and your email promotions, that clearly communicates any such disclaimers.</text><pictures>None</pictures><Response>{'time': 1565624482840, 'text': "Adam, we are very sorry that your experiences haven't been positive and would welcome the ability to see what we could do for you. <Text>My friend invited my over to Fresh Brothers Pizza last night and we had a blast! There were about 10 of us and it was a great way to catch up with old friends, meet new people and eat LOTS AND LOTS OF PIZZA!

I would like to thank Debbie Goldberg for being the hostess with the mostess! She made sure that our drinks were always full and most importantly she made sure that our rather large party had plenty to eat.

Mission Accomplished!!  It has been 12 hours since I ate any food and I am still in a Pizza Coma!

So lets talk about the Fresh Brothers location itself. It is Hollywood so there is a lot of traffic and the spots in the parking lot go quickly. I rode my bike so I was able to park right in front.

This place has a lot of tv's. When I was done counting them, I found two more in the bathroom so I think the total is like 15 flatscreens for a pretty small location. I thought it was awesome! They have two tv's that point outside so you can watch tv if you are standing in front of the building.. Even more awesome!

The food was awesome. Let me take you through what I ate:

We had the fresh knots and wings. The knots were very good and they are described like this. Garlic bread tied in tasty knots, dusted with parmesan, pizza sauce on the side

After the appetizers came out, then came out the salads. I dove into the BBQ Chicken Salad  and it was very yummy. It was very fresh and here are the ingredients for that. Barbecued chicken breast over a tasty bed of romaine, cheddar cheese, corn, zesty onions and black beans topped with fried onions.

The final course was the pizzas and there was plenty to go around. To be honest, I don't know how many kinds of pizza's were out there but they were all called. My friend Dimple has a custom pizza made for her which has Sausage, Pepperoni and Red Onions on it. I think I might have liked it the best. I hope to see the Dimple Special on the menu sometime soon..

The Bottom Line: The food here is awesome and they have 10 locations throughout Los Angeles. I would recommend trying any of them!</Text><pictures>None< /pictures><response>None<//response>< Gmap_id>

<Review>Healthy food with a Korean American leaning.
Lean in to Wildflower Cafe. It's no nonsense & you get really delicious, healthy food.
Isn't it typically difficult to find any of these characteristics at an eaterie?
Not @ Wildflower cafe.
I recall the son of the owner working here. He was a lean, good-looking young man. He didn't want a cafe serving unhealthy food. He was an athlete.

The decor inside was really cool. The music was loud (maybe it was so that when it was really busy it would be backround music. But it was just us 2 and we couldn't hear each other speak.

the ultimate ice cream experience.

< Text>
Probably the best Cabo location. If you can snag a table on the deck upstairs, you get a really nice view of the beach. The last time I went was Sunday of Labor Day weekend. It wasn't overcrowded, so it was enjoyable. Prior to that, I had always gone at varying times on Saturday. In my Saturday experience, it is always too crowded, and I'm left standing in the way until my friends and I can swoop in on a table. The margaritas aren't bad, but coming from a margarita connoisseur, they are nothing to write home about. They do have a variety of fun flavors, though. And if size is your thing, this is your place.</Text>

<review>PLEASE! Read your RECEIPT!!

This is coming from a customer who has been to this and MANY Cabo Cantina's and I believe they are trained to skim (not scam) the customers.

They literally take your order with a smile, then serve you whatever drink they want. OR They serve you what you order and add El DORADO to the bill. El Dorado is the premium drink that is $12.95 or $13.95 depending on how they decide to bill it (or their fancy keying or renaming it to another, cheaper drink). I ALWAYS order the TJ classic which is $7.95 and the most basic Jose Cuervo Margarita.

They will charge for the El Dorado (Patron tequila) margarita and say they made a mistake if you challenge it. Then, instead of changing that, they offer to remove a food item (for alcohol billing and for skimming purposes) instead of adjusting the real price of the drinks you ORDERED.  They will say the price difference (b/c its not listed on the menu) is only $1 or $2 but as you can see, its $5 or $6!

In the End, ALWAYS check your receipt.  Do NOT pay for drinks misattributed to your bill. And, do NOT let them take advantage of you, because as long as I have been going there, THEY WILL ALWAYS TRY!.

I have been going there for over 11 years, and Everytime, EVERY location, they try the same skim (scam) and everytime I catch them, call them out, and get my bill adjusted!

Do the SAME!< /review></record>

<Review>If you are looking for a place to drink next to the beach with less than ridiculous pricing, than this is a decent option. Well, pretty good considering it's one of only a few options.

Their margaritas are insanely sweet, even the classic. Also, please note that pricing on drinks can be a bit deceptive, especially during happy hour.

Food on the other hand is surprisingly good. Flavorful and in pretty generous portions, this is definitely not a good place for a diet but great with a beer or two.

Service is pretty unresponsive, so it isn't a great place if you're in a rush. But if you're afternoon or evening is relaxed, it's not a bad place to spend some time.</Review>< Pics>

<user_name>Elizabeth Trejo<//user_name>< date>
1415834348696< /date>
< Rating>
4</Rating>
<text>For several years now I've been coming to this Cabo Cantina every so often. Mostly to watch sports and have some of their giant margaritas. I finally went to their Taco Tuesday and I was very impressed!

I've never liked their food much (I'm Mexican, I know what authentic Mexican food should taste like), but the margaritas are great along with other drinks. The decor and atmosphere is very fun and young. They have an upstairs and downstairs area, both with outside patios. Located right off the Venice Beach Boardwalk, it is the perfect location for "drinks on the beach" (you can't literally drink on the beach, unfortunately, but you catch my flow).

Taco Tuesday was great! I was worried about trying the tacos but once they were on the table I was excited to try them! Not disapointed at all; they were really delicious, at least the steak and chicken ones I had were. They had plenty of meat and came with a side of mexican rice and black beans. Paired up with a giant margarita, Taco Tuesday was perfect here! It was a full house for the Happy Hour which goes from 4pm-10pm, everyone enjoying a conversation over sports, food, and drinks.

Since it gets really busy, service isn't as quick but thats understandable. All the servers are very nice. I've never had a issue with customer service here. Parking sucks, but if you are lucky you might just get a meter right outside or there is also valet across the street and a parking lot at the end of the street.<//text><pics>None</pics><resp>None<//resp><Gmap_id>0x80c2ba8e401b2d1d:0x924fbf79ef48be8c< /Gmap_id></record>

< text>
You really can't miss Cabo Cantina when walking on the street here because of the crowd and the general rukus (popular here). I found Cabo to be true to my other Cabo experience in Pacific Beach (party town numero uno). If you like this type of energy then this will be your vehicle of happiness.

Surprisingly the overall ratings are only 3.5. My question is how can a place be this popular, crowded most of the time and get this low of a rating. Perhaps those that enjoy the vibe are not the type to do a review (ever think of that). Sometimes the most demonstrative visitor is someone that may have had an off experience. They almost always give the lowest 1 Star rating; when in general they should expect to have some attitude because of the mix of alcohol and average tolerance to the spirits.

By:
cmilton111
2017
Google Guide</text>

<pictures>None<//pictures>< text>
I barely write reviews because I dnt wanna take the time to talk about a place unless it really deserves it. I have never been to a place that treats you with such disrespect. This cabo cantina needs to take some pointers from the other locations like the one in West Hollywood.  I get it it's like the "Mexican style" bar and grill so you don't expect much. But you should at least be treated like a customer. First the blended Mega Margarita that I split with my friends was really icy. It taste like a slurpee from 7 11 that was really watered down. Way to much ice. I coulnt even taste the flavor I got let alone the alcohol. But I drank it anyway. Didn't bother to tell the server. We also got nachos which was great. Then I ordered buy one get one Margarita on ice which was really good. The problem didn't really come until we got the bill. The server (I dnt know her name but seems to be a dark hair white girl)  wrote 20% of 100 =$20 on the ticket. I'm a server my friends are servers so we felt really disrespected at the fact that she wrote it on the bill. Like we were going to do it anyway because we are of the industry but she didn't have to write it on the bill. We felt because we are a diverse group of minorities she had a need to write it on the bill. Some restaurants have the percentages PRINTED at the bottom for your convenience, but she flat out wrote it with her pen. When we asked her about it she brushed it off and said it was a bad habit. So then we start to wonder if this is policy so we called a manager( a seemingly white male named Guy )over. Before he came I saw her debrief him of what happen (which was really nothing). When he came he seem to already know what he was gonna say. When we asked him if it's policy he said yes because we have a lot of tourists come here. Then I said tourist are not you shouldn't try to force tip out of pple. Then he said its policy and its not going to change. And then said every cabo cantina is different.  I thought to myself yes every one is different, they aren't racist. The manager NAMED GUY was very rude. When I asked him for his name he said it was Guy and then he asked for mine and I said no. Which seem to really piss him off. It then Looked like he gestured to security to kick us out. They didn't get a chance to we were leaving anyway. My thing is you never know who you are going to get we were going to tip 20% anyway. Because of the manager we tipped her NOTHING. She wasnt a good server anyway. The team is only as good as the leader and the leader sucks. Not coming here again. I'll stick to what I know.< /text>
